# cs.DB [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Efficient and Effective In-place Graph-based Vector Index Updates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15576)
*Haotian Liu,Yujun He,Bo Tang*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: 提出了Yi系统，通过分解促进整合的设计理念，实现了基于图向量的高效原地更新，在保持高召回率的同时显著提升了更新吞吐量和并发搜索吞吐量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大语言模型时代，向量需要频繁更新以捕捉实时信息，但现有方法存在矛盾：基于聚类的向量索引方法更新吞吐量高但搜索结果质量低，而基于图的向量索引方法虽然质量高但更新吞吐量差（需要定期合并更新批次）。

Method: 提出Yi系统，核心思想是"分解促进整合"。具体包括三个核心组件：(1) 基于tasklet的执行引擎，(2) 异步缓冲区管理器，(3) 向量文件系统。通过向量级别的更新机制实现原地更新。

Result: 在800M数据集上，Yi相比最先进系统实现了1.75倍的更新吞吐量和1.8倍的并发搜索吞吐量提升，同时仅使用73%的峰值内存和更少的CPU核心。

Conclusion: Yi成功实现了基于图的向量索引的高效原地更新，兼顾了高更新吞吐量和良好的搜索结果质量，证明了分解促进整合的设计理念在向量数据系统中的有效性。

Abstract: In the era of Large Language Models (LLMs), efficient vector updates are critical for capturing real-time information from rapidly evolving data. However, it is not trivial to process frequent vector insert and delete updates and maintain a high recall of the search results simultaneously. Specifically, the cluster-based vector indexing methods have high update throughput but low search result quality. Existing out-of-place graph-based vector indexing update approaches suffer from poor update throughput due to the need to periodically merge update batches into the underlying graph index.
  Building a vector data system that supports efficient and effective in-place updates is inherently challenging. In this work, we propose Yi to achieve it. In particular, Yi supports in-place graph-based vector indexing updates with consistently high update throughput and good search result quality. The key idea of Yi is decomposition facilitates consolidation. In particular, we introduce a vector-level update mechanism and architect Yi with three core components: (i) a tasklet-based execution engine, (ii) an asynchronous buffer manager, and (iii) a vector file system. Experimental results demonstrate that Yi achieves 1.75x higher update throughput and 1.8x higher concurrent search throughput than the state-of-the-art systems on the 800M dataset, while using only 73% of the peak memory and fewer CPU cores.

</details>


### [2] [Verifying Isolation Levels of Database Implementations for Free Using Separation Logic](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15877)
*Anders Alnor Mathiasen,Amin Timany,Lars Birkedal*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于分离逻辑规范的形式化验证方法，用于证明数据库实现确实提供了其声称的隔离级别。该方法通过从分离逻辑规范中直接推导隔离级别，考虑所有可能的程序执行，并利用Rocq证明助手进行了机械化证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数据库隔离级别的正确实现至关重要，但现有的测试方法只能发现问题，无法提供形式化保证。缺乏一种形式化验证方法，确保数据库实现与所声称的隔离级别一致。

Method: 从分离逻辑规范的结构中直接推导隔离级别，将隔离级别形式化为事务一致性模型。通过对数据库操作进行分离逻辑验证，得到"自由定理"：任何满足特定分离逻辑规范的实现都自动满足相应的隔离级别。所有证明在Rocq证明助手中机械化实现。

Result: 提出了一个形式化验证方法，能够证明任意数据库实现（在与任意客户端交互的所有可能执行下）确实实现了其声明的隔离级别。

Conclusion: 该工作提高了数据库鲁棒性的可达成标准，为数据库实现的形式化保证提供了新范式。

Abstract: Modern databases are highly concurrent and provide transactions as a mean of grouping several database operations into atomically applied units. Database vendors and software engineers use isolation levels to describe the consistency guarantees of transactions. The popular isolation levels give weak guarantees, with intricate semantics, to optimize performance of applications. The problem of assuring that database implementations actually implement the isolation level guarantees that application developers build their systems upon has received a great deal of attention from the testing community. But until now, there exists no method for formally verifying that a database implementation actually implements the isolation level that database vendors says it provides. In this paper, we present a method for verifying that a database implements an isolation level: we derive isolation levels directly, as formalized in transactional consistency models by the database community, from the structure of separation logic specifications. By doing so, we consider all program executions that a database and arbitrary clients of the database could produce. The result is a so-called free theorem meaning that any database implementation, whose operations are verified against a specific set of separation logic specifications, actually implements its isolation level. As all proofs in this paper are mechanized in the Rocq proof assistant and build upon a detailed semantic model of program execution, we believe this contribution raises the bar for the achievable robustness of databases.

</details>


<div id='cs.DC'></div>

# cs.DC [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [FSZ: Breaking the Prediction-Throughput Trade-off in GPU Lossy Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15413)
*Jiajun Huang*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: FSZ是一种GPU有损压缩器，通过跨块预测、自适应多阶预测和单通四路评估三种协同创新，在单CUDA内核中同时实现了更高的压缩比和吞吐量，在NVIDIA GH200上压缩比最高提升10.95倍，吞吐量达676 GB/s（压缩）和785 GB/s（解压）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GPU快速有损压缩器（如cuSZp系列）虽然通过纯GPU单内核设计实现了高吞吐量，但压缩率受限，因为它们通常在独立块上应用固定的一阶预测器，未能充分利用数据间相关性。

Method: FSZ提出了三种相互强化的算法创新：（1）跨块预测状态传递——在256元素块边界间传递Lorenzo预测状态，消除7/8边界残差；（2）每块自适应多阶预测与中心化——从一阶、二阶及中心化变体中自适应选择最优策略；（3）单通四路评估——利用有限差分的数学性质，在单次数据读取中评估所有变体，不增加带宽开销。

Result: 在NVIDIA GH200上使用8个真实数据集，FSZ压缩比相比cuSZp-P提升高达10.95倍，相比SOTA方法cuSZp-O提升高达2.92倍；同时实现最高平均吞吐量（压缩676 GB/s，解压785 GB/s），无性能损失。

Conclusion: FSZ证明通过巧妙设计预测阶段的多项算法创新，可以在不牺牲吞吐量的前提下大幅提升GPU有损压缩的压缩比，为科学计算数据的高效压缩提供了新方向。

Abstract: Existing fast GPU error-bounded lossy compressors have achieved high throughput through pure-GPU single-kernel designs, but their compression ratios remain limited because they typically apply a fixed first-order predictor on independent blocks. We propose FSZ, a GPU error-bounded lossy compressor that redesigns the prediction stage with three mutually reinforcing algorithmic innovations to achieve both higher compression ratios and higher throughput within a single CUDA kernel: (1) cross-block prediction state carries Lorenzo prediction state across block boundaries within 256-element tiles, eliminating 7 out of 8 boundary residuals that inflate encoding rates; (2) per-tile adaptive multi-order prediction and centering adaptively selects the best compression strategy per tile from first-order, second-order, and centering variants; and (3) a single-pass four-way evaluation exploits a mathematical property of finite differences to evaluate all variants from a single data read, enabling richer prediction within the same bandwidth budget as a fixed predictor. Experiments on NVIDIA GH200 GPU with 8 real-world application datasets show that FSZ outperforms cuSZp-P by up to 10.95x and the state-of-the-art cuSZp-O by up to 2.92x in compression ratio. Notably, these gains come with no throughput penalty: FSZ simultaneously achieves the highest average throughput (676 GB/s compression, 785 GB/s decompression) among all evaluated compressors.

</details>


### [4] [Scalable LLM Agent Tool Access in the Cloud](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15593)
*Mingxin Li,Enge Song,Yueshang Zuo,Xiaodong Liu,Rong Wen,Qiang Fu,Gianni Antichi,Jian He,Jing Tie,Zhou Shao,Xiaobo Xue,Xiong Xiao,Luyao Zhong,Shaokai Zhang,Jiangu Zhao,Jianyuan Lu,Shize Zhang,Xiaoqing Sun,Changgang Zheng,Zihao Fan,Haonan Li,Tian Pan,Xiaomin Wu,Yang Song,Xing Li,Biao Lyu,Meng Li,Haipeng Dai,Guihai Chen,Shunmin Zhu*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种面向MCP（模型上下文协议）的云规模网关系统，通过将遗留服务集成、协议兼容、访问控制、工具推荐和会话感知路由等功能卸载至网关，打破直连模型，实现工具访问规模扩展至3000+，同时将工具选择时间降低8.9倍、Token使用量降低23.8倍，混合检索保持98%的Top-15召回率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MCP已成为LLM智能体工具调用的事实标准接口，但在云规模部署下存在两大痛点：1）工具提供方：遗留服务无法直接通过MCP调用，协议快速演进带来兼容性成本；2）智能体侧：LLM上下文窗口和推理开销限制了可访问工具数量，大规模工具集会增加Token消耗、推理延迟并降低任务成功率。此外，有状态MCP后端的多副本部署还需要维护会话亲和性，增加了客户端复杂性。

Method: 提出了一个云规模MCP网关系统，在数据平面打破直连模型，将以下功能卸载至网关：遗留服务集成、不兼容MCP变体的整合、访问控制、工具推荐（采用混合检索实现98% Top-15召回率）以及会话感知路由。该设计将工具选择从LLM侧解耦，通过混合检索技术实现3000+工具的高效选择。

Result: 混合检索实现98% Top-15召回率；支持3000+工具的高精度选择；工具选择时间降低8.9倍；Token使用量降低23.8倍；每次调用开销低且具有良好的扩展稳定性。

Conclusion: 该网关系统有效解决了MCP在云规模部署中的可扩展性和兼容性问题，显著提升了工具选择效率，并已在生产环境中部署验证。文中还分享了实际部署中的经验教训。

Abstract: LLM agents increasingly rely on tool calling to act on external systems, and the Model Context Protocol (MCP) has quickly become its de facto interface. Operating MCP at cloud scale, however, becomes difficult. On the tool provider side, legacy services are not directly callable through MCP; the rapid protocol development also creates ongoing compatibility cost. On the agent side, the number of accessible tool is limited by the LLM context window and inference overhead; mounting a large tool set increases token usage and inference latency and can reduce task success rate. Moreover, for stateful MCP backends with multiple replicas, preserving session affinity increases client-side complexity.
  We present a cloud-scale gateway system for MCP service. It breaks the direct-connect model on the data plane and offloads legacy service integration, consolidating incompatible MCP variants, access control, tool recommendation, and session-aware routing to the gateway. Hybrid retrieval sustains 98% Top-15 recall; it scales agent tool access to 3,000+ with high tool selection accuracy, and reduces tool selection time by $8.9\times$ and token usage by $23.8\times$, with low per-call overhead, stable under scale-out. Finally, we share the lessons learned from deploying the gateway system in production.

</details>


### [5] [JoyNexus: Service-Oriented Multi-Tenant Post-Training for VLA Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16074)
*Haoran Sun,Wentao Zhang,Junyang Hua,Hedan Yang,Yongjian Guo,Yifei Zhang,Xiaolong Xiang,Mingxi Luo,Jing Long,Chen Zhao,Chen Zhou,Wanting Xu,Qiming Yang,Hui Zhang,Song Wang,Xiaodong Bai,Shuai Di,Xu Chu,Xiaotie Deng,Yicheng Gong,Junwu Xiong*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: JoyNexus 是一个面向多租户 VLA（视觉-语言-动作）模型后训练的统一服务平台，通过解耦训练、推理和环境服务，利用共享基模型和租户专属槽位，结合全局调度与分组批处理技术，实现跨租户资源共享，降低 GPU 时间开销并提升服务利用率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有后训练服务（如 GPU 租赁或批处理作业）为单租户独占资源，导致用户需自行处理基础设施适配，且短任务或突发任务在按卡时计费模式下成本高昂，同时服务提供方的资源利用率低下。

Method: JoyNexus 将训练模型服务、推理模型服务和环境服务解耦，均通过 API 访问，背后基于共享基模型+租户专属槽位；租户可调用高级语义 API 或自定义算法；多租户并发提交任务，动作模块、优化器等隔离，由全局训练队列和推理队列调度；并提出分组批处理技术，对共享模型前缀的异构 VLA 数据执行单次骨干网络前向传播。

Result: 相比隔离的单租户执行，JoyNexus 通过跨租户调度共享资源，降低了总 GPU 时间，提升了服务利用率。

Conclusion: JoyNexus 有效解决了 VLA 后训练中资源独占带来的成本与效率问题，为多租户场景提供了一种统一、高效的服务架构。

Abstract: The post-training of Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models is essential due to the diversity of simulators, robot embodiments, and task objectives. Existing compute services, whether offered as direct accelerator rental or batch-workload submission, typically allocate an exclusive set of GPU and CPU resources to a single tenant. While this paradigm maximizes client flexibility, it burdens users with infrastructure adaptation, and the fixed card-hour accounting model renders short or bursty workloads both expensive for tenants and inefficient for the service provider. To address these challenges, we present JoyNexus, a unified service for multi-tenant VLA supervised fine-tuning, reinforcement learning, and evaluation. JoyNexus decouples the Training Model Service, Inference Model Service, and Environment Service, each accessed through APIs and backed by resident shared base models with tenant-specific slots. Tenants can directly invoke high-level semantic APIs for training, rollout, and evaluation, or compose custom algorithms using lower-level APIs and their assigned endpoints. Multiple tenants submit workloads concurrently; their action modules, optimizers, rollout records, and policy versions remain isolated, and the service is scheduled by the global Training Queue and Inference Queue. To further improve multi-tenant training efficiency, JoyNexus introduces group batching for heterogeneous VLA data schemas that share a compatible model-facing prefix, enabling a single shared backbone forward pass over grouped samples. Finally, we evaluate JoyNexus through workload simulation and a group-batching pipeline in a realistic embodied scenario. Results show that, compared with isolated single-tenant execution, JoyNexus reduces aggregate GPU time and improves service utilization via cross-tenant scheduling on shared resources.

</details>


### [6] [Every Microsecond Matters: Achieving Near Speed-of-Light Latency in GPU Collectives](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16100)
*Siyuan Shen,Anton Korzh,John Bachan,Tiancheng Chen,Arnav Goel,Ludwig Schneider,Pouya Kousha,Zhenhao He,Sylvain Jeaugey,Kamil Iskra,Nishank Chandawala,Jeff R. Hammond,Torsten Hoefler*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文针对GPU集体通信中延迟敏感型工作负载（如长上下文LLM推理）的问题，提出了接近硬件光速下界的优化方案，通过无屏障同步、对称内存与多播技术，在NCCL设备端API上构建自定义集体内核，实现小中消息延迟降低至绝对SoL下界的7%以内，并在LLM推理和传统HPC任务中验证了性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GPU集体通信主要优化带宽，但新兴负载（如长上下文LLM推理）受限于延迟，微秒级开销即影响性能与成本，亟需接近硬件光速下界的低延迟设计。

Method: 提出三条关键原则：无屏障同步、对称内存高效利用、多播技术。基于NCCL设备端API构建低延迟自定义集体内核，实现新的对称集体通信操作。

Result: 微基准测试中，小中消息延迟降至绝对SoL下界的7%以内；集成到实际应用后，改善LLM推理的token间延迟与吞吐量，并加速cuSOLVERMp。

Conclusion: 所提优化方法在AI推理和传统HPC负载中均有显著收益，证明了延迟优化对现代GPU集群通信的重要性。

Abstract: GPU collective communication is typically optimized for bandwidth, yet many emerging workloads are increasingly limited by latency. Long-context decode-heavy large language model (LLM) inference is a prime example, where serving large models requires multiple GPUs, and many small collectives lie directly on the critical path of token generation. Therefore, even microsecond of overhead can impact performance and cost. In this work, we study how to approach the hardware Speed-of-Light (SoL) lower bound for GPU collectives within a scale-up network. We identify key principles for near-optimal designs, including barrier-free synchronization and efficient use of symmetric memory and multicast. Building on NCCL's device-side API, we develop low-latency interfaces for constructing custom collective kernels and use them to implement new symmetric collectives in NCCL. Microbenchmarks show substantial latency reductions for small and medium messages, reducing overhead to within 7% of the absolute SoL lower bound. When integrated into real applications, these kernels improve inter-token latency and throughput in LLM inference and accelerate cuSOLVERMp, demonstrating benefits for both AI inference and traditional HPC workloads.

</details>


<div id='cs.DS'></div>

# cs.DS [[Back]](#toc)

### [7] [The Multiple-Choice Matroid Secretary Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15407)
*Matías Ortiz-Angel,José A. Soto*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文研究多选拟阵秘书问题(J,κ)-MSP，提出了分离在线存储与最终可行解的模型。主要结果包括：横向拟阵在无容量限制下的最优精确算法（概率竞争比等于经典J选秘书问题的最优成功概率）；带容量横向拟阵的单阈值路由算法；以及多轨道方法在k-列稀疏拟阵和基于并的方法在分层拟阵中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典秘书问题只能选一个候选人，而实际场景（如招聘、资源分配）需要选择多个候选人，且可能有容量约束和拟阵结构限制。现有研究缺乏将在线存储与最终可行解分离的通用框架。

Method: 提出(J,κ)-MSP框架，将在线存储（在J重并拟阵中维护可行候选池AUX，容量限制|AUX|≤κ·rank(M)）与最终提取最大权独立集分开。设计了两种实现：多轨道算法（维护J个独立集）和基于并的算法（直接在J重并拟阵中维护池）。

Result: 1. 对横向拟阵在(J,∞)下给出最优算法，概率竞争比等于经典J选秘书问题最优成功率，且随J指数收敛到1；2. 对带容量横向拟阵给出单阈值路由算法，分析有限参数界和渐近公式；3. 多轨道方法对k-列稀疏拟阵保证1-O(e^{-J/(ke)})；基于并方法对分层拟阵保证1-O(e^{-J/e})。

Conclusion: 本文提出的框架成功将经典秘书问题推广到多选拟阵场景，揭示了秩一实例是横向拟阵类的最坏情况，并展示了不同算法范式在不同拟阵结构下的性能保证。

Abstract: We introduce and study the multiple-choice matroid secretary problem, denoted $(J,κ)$-MSP. For rank-one matroids and $κ=\infty$, it reduces to the classical secretary problem with $J$ choices. Elements arrive in uniformly random order. Algorithms may keep a candidate pool $\mathrm{AUX}$ feasible in the $J$-fold union matroid $\mathcal{M}^{(J)}$ satisfying $|\mathrm{AUX}|\le κ\cdot\mathrm{rank}(\mathcal{M})$. Finally, one extracts the maximum-weight independent subset of $\mathrm{AUX}$ in $\mathcal{M}$. This model separates online storage from the final feasible solution. We study two multiple-choice implementations: multi-track algorithms (maintaining $J$ independent sets of $\mathcal{M}$) and union-based algorithms (maintaining the pool directly in $\mathcal{M}^{(J)}$).
  Our main result is an exact optimal algorithm for transversal matroids in the uncapacitated $(J,\infty)$ setting. For fixed $J$, its probability-competitive ratio equals the optimal success probability of the classical $J$-choice secretary problem. Thus, rank-one instances are the worst case for the whole transversal class, and the optimal guarantee converges exponentially fast to $1$ as $J$ grows. We also analyze a simple single-threshold routing algorithm for capacitated transversal matroids with local capacities $b$ and global capacity $κ\cdot\mathrm{rank}(\mathcal{M})$. Its analysis provides explicit finite-parameter bounds and asymptotic formulas, showing how finite-rank loss caused by global capacity decays, and how $b$, $J$, and $κ$ interact. Finally, we instantiate the multi-track approach for $k$-column-sparse matroids (guarantee $1-O(e^{-J/(ke)})$) and the union-based approach for laminar matroids (guarantee $1-O(e^{-J/e})$).

</details>


### [8] [The k-Sum Lateness Problem on a Single Machine](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15462)
*Ricardo Arancibia-Castillo,José A. Soto*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文研究单机调度中最小化前k大延误值问题，证明其弱NP完全性，给出固定k的O(k²n^{k+2})算法，提出块-岛分解结构，并发展出FPT算法、伪多项式算法和全多项式近似方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在经典调度理论中，最大延误（k=1）和总延误（k=n）是两种极端目标，但实际生产中管理者往往更关心最严重的若干延误而非全部延误。该问题桥接了这两种极端情形，Woeginger曾对top-k延误问题提出猜想，本文旨在解决该猜想并填补调度理论中这一空白。

Method: （1）通过归约证明决策版本弱NP完全性；（2）针对固定k设计动态规划算法；（3）提出块-岛分解结构：最优调度中，非top-k作业按到期日形成块，top-k作业在同类到期日中构成SPT序后缀；（4）利用对偶表示将问题转化为系列总延误实例，发展伪多项式算法和FPTAS。

Result: （1）当k为输入时决策问题弱NP完全；（2）固定k时O(k² n^{k+2})算法；（3）参数化D+k的FPT算法；（4）全多项式近似方案，误差≤εM；（5）固定P或固定D的XP算法。

Conclusion: 本文从计算复杂性、精确算法、近似算法和结构刻画多个维度完整刻画了最小化前k大延误问题，解决了Woeginger猜想，并为调度理论中这类"截断型"目标函数提供了通用的分析框架。

Abstract: We study a single-machine scheduling problem in which each job $j$ has a nonnegative processing time $p_j\ge 0$ and a due date $d_j\in\mathbb{R}$. For a non-idling schedule $S$, let $C_j(S)$ be the completion time and let $L_j(S)=C_j(S)-d_j$ be the (possibly negative) lateness. The objective is to minimize the sum of the $k$ largest lateness values, interpolating between maximum lateness ($k=1$) and total lateness ($k=n$).
  We prove that the decision version is weakly NP-complete when $k$ is part of the input. For fixed $k$, we give an $O(k^2 n^{k+2})$ algorithm. As a consequence, we resolve a conjecture of Woeginger on the top-$k$ tardiness problem and obtain an $O(n^{k+2})$ algorithm for every fixed $k$.
  Our main structural result shows that there exists an optimal schedule that admits a block-island decomposition. Outside a suitable top-$k$ set, jobs form due-date blocks ordered by due date. Within each due-date class, the top-$k$ jobs form a suffix in lexicographic shortest-processing-time (SPT) order. This structure also yields an FPT algorithm parameterized by $D+k$, where $D$ is the number of distinct due dates.
  Independently, a standard dual representation of the top-$k$ objective reduces the problem to a family of total-tardiness instances with uniformly shifted due dates. For integral data, this gives a pseudopolynomial algorithm and a fully polynomial additive approximation scheme with error at most $\varepsilon M$, where $M=\max\{1,\max_j p_j,\max_j |d_j|\}$. The same route also gives XP algorithms for fixed $P$ and fixed $D$, where $P$ is the number of distinct processing times.

</details>


### [9] [A Study of Parallelizable Alternatives to Dynamic Time Warping for Aligning Long Sequences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15478)
*Daniel Yang,Thaxter Shaw,TJ Tsai*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文提出四种并行化对齐算法替代DTW，利用GPU等硬件加速长序列对齐，其中ParDTW在保持精确对齐的同时将运行时间降低1.5-2个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工作主要聚焦降低DTW的总计算量或内存开销，但未能充分利用GPU等并行硬件来减少实际运行时间（wall clock time）。

Method: 提出四种并行化对齐算法：前三种通过将代价矩阵分割为矩形区域并行处理来近似DTW；第四种沿对角线并行处理代价矩阵以实现精确DTW对齐。最终选出两种最优算法WSDTW和ParDTW并实现GPU版本。

Result: ParDTW性能最佳：计算精确DTW对齐，在长序列上相比现有方法运行时间减少1.5-2个数量级。

Abstract: This article investigates several parallelizable alternatives to DTW for estimating the alignment between two long sequences. Whereas most previous work has focused on reducing the total computation and/or memory costs of DTW, our focus is instead on reducing wall clock time by utilizing common hardware like GPUs that are optimized for parallel processing. We propose and study four different parallelizable alignment algorithms: the first three algorithms compute approximations of DTW by breaking the pairwise cost matrix into rectangular regions and processing the regions in parallel, and the fourth algorithm computes an exact DTW alignment by processing the cost matrix along diagonals rather than rows or columns. We characterize the performance of our proposed alignment algorithms on an audio-audio alignment task, and we develop GPU-based implementations for the two best-performing algorithms, which we call weakly-ordered Segmental DTW (WSDTW) and Parallelized Diagonal DTW (ParDTW). Our experiments indicate that ParDTW is the most practical and useful of the four algorithms: it computes an exact DTW alignment and reduces runtime by 1.5 to 2 orders of magnitude on long sequences compared to current alternatives. We present a comprehensive evaluation and study of the alignment accuracy, runtime, and practical limitations of the proposed alignment algorithms.

A representative task is to use samples from an unknown distribution $P$ over a very large domain to decide between two cases: $P = P_{\mathsf{ref}}$ for a fixed reference distribution $P_{\mathsf{ref}}$, or there exists a distinguisher $f$ in a bounded class $\mathcal{F}$ which witnesses the separation $|\mathbf{E}_P[f] - \mathbf{E}_{P_{\mathsf{ref}}}[f]| > ε$. This is the task of identity testing with respect to fooling distance, a name inspired by the conceptual connection with pseudorandomness. (Formally, our model instantiates integral probability metrics from Boolean classes of bounded expressivity.)
  We show that testing with respect to fooling distance is not only a natural computational problem that admits sample-efficient algorithms even in high-dimensional settings, but also one that reveals and underlies connections between three seemingly unrelated areas of study: testable learning, verification of learning algorithms, and testing of structured distributions (whose "$\mathcal{A}_k$-testing" model our framework extends). These connections yield new results for all of these models, including:
  1. Testable proper learners using membership queries for halfspaces and decision trees.
  2. A lower bound for testable PAC verification in terms of Rademacher complexity, and a distribution-free verification protocol for disjoint unions of $k$ multidimensional rectangles.
  3. Identity testers (with respect to total variation distance) for decision tree distributions and distributions with low-degree polynomial densities, over Boolean and continuous hypercube domains.

### [12] [NP-Hardness of Connected Components Reconfiguration under Component Jumping on Caterpillar Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15737)
*Naoki Kitamura,Seitaro Kawaguchi,Yuya Terashima,Taisuke Izumi*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Nakahata等人提出的CCRCJ问题在弦图上的多重集大小约束的复杂度尚未解决，本文旨在填补这一理论空白。

Method: 1) 通过归约证明CCRCJ在毛毛虫图上NP-hard；2) 设计基于数据结构的O(n log n)路径图决策算法；3) 在足够大空白空间下给出O(n log n)长度的重构序列构造方法。

Result: 1) 证明CCRCJ在毛毛虫图上NP-hard，进而推出弦图多重集版本NP-hard；2) 路径图决策算法从O(n²)改进到O(n log n)；3) 存在O(n log n)长度的重构序列且可高效输出。

Abstract: We study the Connected Components Reconfiguration problem (CCR), in which connected components on a graph are transformed according to a specified reconfiguration rule. CCR generalizes Independent Set Reconfiguration by treating tokens not as individual vertices but as connected components of prescribed sizes. Among the variants of CCR, we focus on the component-jumping model, denoted by \CCRCJ. Nakahata.\ introduced this problem and showed that the decision problem for \CCRCJ~can be solved in $O(n^2)$ time on path graphs for arbitrary component sizes, and in polynomial time on chordal graphs when all connected components have the same size. However, the complexity on chordal graphs under a multiset size constraint remained open.
  In this paper, we study this multiset version of \CCRCJ~from both complexity-theoretic and algorithmic viewpoints. First, we prove that \CCRCJ~is NP-hard even on caterpillar graphs, which is a very restricted subclass of trees and chordal graphs minimally above path graphs. This result immediately implies NP-hardness for chordal graphs under a multiset size constraint, thereby resolving Nakahata's open problem on chordal graphs under multiset size constraints. Second, we revisit \CCRCJ~on path graphs. We improve the previous $O(n^2)$-time algorithm for the decision problem by giving an $O(n\log n)$-time decision algorithm. Moreover, when the instance has sufficiently large empty space, we show that there exists a reconfiguration sequence of length $O(n\log n)$, and such a sequence can be output efficiently.

### [13] [Contextual Fraction on Permutation Gain Graphs: Exact Algorithms, Query Lower Bounds, and Dynamic Maintenance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16037)
*Ronald Katende*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 论文发现了一类"排列-运输"结构，在该类中，经验模型的不兼容分数（contextual fraction）计算可简化为不动点计算，实现了查询最优和动态维护的高效算法，并与CSP的Bulatov-Zhuk二分法建立了联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 一般情境下，判断经验模型的contextual fraction是否严格小于1是NP完全的，且标准线性规划依赖于指数级规模的全局赋值列。作者希望找到一类可高效计算的子问题，并研究其计算复杂度边界。

Method: 定义排列-传输增益图及其holonomy子群H，利用H的不动点集F和H不变根分布p，推导出NCF(e)=p(F)的闭式公式；给出O(|O|(|V|+|E|))时间算法；基于排列-表查询模型证明下界Ω((|O|-1)|E|)；设计支持边插入/删除的O(|O|)动态维护方案；最后将CF<1问题与有限域CSP问题建立多项式时间等价。

Result: 1) 排列-传输类中contextual fraction有精确闭式解；2) 算法在查询模型下达到最优（常数因子内）；3) 支持动态维护，弦插入/删除O(|O|)时间，兼容性及CF查询O(1)；4) 二进制约束语言下，CF<1与CSP问题等价，继承Bulatov-Zhuk二分法。

Conclusion: 论文识别了一个可查询最优且可动态维护的易处理性"岛屿"，该结果既刻画了contextual fraction问题的计算复杂度边界，也通过CSP联系揭示了其表达能力的理论极限。

Abstract: For an explicitly represented finite empirical model, deciding whether the contextual fraction is strictly below one is NP-complete, while the standard exact linear program has one column for every global assignment. We identify a permutation-transport class in which this global problem collapses to a fixed-point calculation. Let a connected permutation gain graph act on a finite state set $O$, let $H \leq{ \rm Sym}(O)$ be its holonomy subgroup, let $F = {\rm Fix}(H)$, and let $p$ be an $H$-invariant root distribution. For the induced empirical model, \[ {\rm NCF}(e)=p(F),\qquad {\rm CF}(e)=1-p(F). \] Consequently, compatibility, $F$, and ${\rm CF}(e)$ are computable in $O(|O|(|V|+|E|))$ arithmetic and table operations. For every finite simple $2$-edge-connected graph, any deterministic exact algorithm in the explicit permutation-table query model requires at least $(|O|-1)|E|$ probes in the worst case, making the dependence on the input tables optimal up to constant factors. With a fixed spanning tree, chord insertions and deletions require $O(|O|)$ worst-case time, or time proportional to the moved-set representation, while compatibility and contextual-fraction queries take $O(1)$ time. Finally, for common-marginal realizable binary constraint languages, the support threshold ${\rm CF} < 1$ is polynomial-time equivalent to the associated finite-domain constraint-satisfaction problem and therefore inherits the Bulatov--Zhuk dichotomy. The results identify a query-optimal and dynamically maintainable tractability island inside the general contextual-fraction problem.

### [14] [Solving Stackelberg Vertex Cover on trees using split and join](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16078)
*Dominik Scheder,Johannes Tantow*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文研究Stackelberg Vertex Cover问题，提出了三种树结构上的新算法：基于整数权重的伪多项式算法、针对特殊树（P顶点集合在最近公共祖先下封闭）的强多项式算法，以及以F顶点可达P顶点数为参数的FPT算法。这些算法基于一个通过LP对偶和顶点覆盖LP完整性得到的引理，允许在顶点处将实例拆分为多个子实例。此外，引入了"承诺"（commitments）概念，并证明了带承诺的Stackelberg Vertex Cover问题是弱NP完全的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Stackelberg Vertex Cover问题是一个双层优化问题，此前仅知在二部图上NP完全、在路径上可线性时间求解。作者希望扩展可解图类的范围，特别是树结构上的算法设计。

Method: (1) 通过LP对偶和顶点覆盖LP的完整性，推导出一个引理，允许在顶点u处将实例拆分为子实例，要求子实例的最小顶点覆盖在u上一致（都含u或都不含u）；(2) 引入"承诺"概念确保拆分的一致性；(3) 基于该拆分引理，设计了三种树上的算法：伪多项式算法（以最大权重为参数）、针对P顶点在最近公共祖先下封闭的树的强多项式算法、以及以F顶点可达P顶点数为参数的FPT算法。

Result: (1) 提出了树上的伪多项式算法（参数为最大权重，FPT）；(2) 提出了针对特定树（P集合在最近公共祖先下封闭）的强多项式算法；(3) 提出了树上的FPT算法（参数为F顶点可达P顶点数的最大值）；(4) 证明了带承诺的Stackelberg Vertex Cover问题是弱NP完全的。

Conclusion: 通过拆分引理和承诺概念，成功将Stackelberg Vertex Cover问题的可解图类从路径扩展到更广泛的树结构，并刻画了不同树结构下的计算复杂度边界。

Abstract: The Stackelberg Vertex Cover problem is a bilevel optimization problem with two players on a graph $G = (F \cup P, E)$ where each vertex from $F$ has a weight and the first player selects a price for each vertex in $P$. Afterwards, the second player finds a minimum vertex cover $X$ and the first player receives the set price for each vertex from $X \cap P$. The goal is to maximize the revenue of the first player.
  This problem was recently shown to be NP-complete for bipartite graphs while being solvable in linear time on paths. We present three new algorithms for solving Stackelberg Vertex Cover on certain kinds of trees: (1) a pseudo-polynomial algorithm working on general trees when all weights are integer, i.e., it is FPT with the maximum weight as a parameter; (2) a strongly polynomial algorithm for trees having the property that the least common ancestor of any two vertices from $P$ is again in $P$ (this case includes paths); and (3) an FPT-algorithm for trees, where the parameter is the maximum number $P$-vertices $v_i$ that an $F$-vertex $u$ can reach while using no other $P$-vertices.
  These algorithms are based on a lemma that allows us to split instances at a vertex $u$ into multiple sub-instances, which follows from LP duality and integrality of the vertex cover LP on bipartite graphs. The lemma requires that the minimum vertex covers of the sub-instances agree on $u$ (either all include $u$ or all don't). For this we introduce the concept of commitments. Finally, we show that the Stackelberg Vertex Cover problem with commitments is weakly NP-complete.

</details>


### [15] [A Unified Theory of Sparsification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16126)
*Sanjeev Khanna,Aaron Putterman,Madhu Sudan*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种统一的理论框架，用于研究实值编码的稀疏化问题，该框架同时推广了组合稀疏化（如CSP稀疏化）和连续稀疏化（如图谱稀疏化）。核心参数是连续值非冗余度（CVNRD），它捕捉了编码中最大的近似块对角障碍，并证明了基于CVNRD的近似线性大小稀疏化器存在性以及下界约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 组合稀疏化（如CSP稀疏化）与连续稀疏化（如图谱稀疏化）的传统研究方法各不相同，缺乏统一的理论框架。本文旨在提出一种统一的稀疏化理论，能够同时涵盖这两类问题，并揭示其内在的稀疏化障碍机制。

Method: 定义了实值编码C ⊆ ℝ≥0^m的稀疏化问题，引入连续值非冗余度（CVNRD）作为核心参数，它度量了编码中最大的近似块对角结构。基于该参数，设计了一种能够生成近似线性大小稀疏化器的构造方法，并证明了对于一大类坐标方向上无偏的随机稀疏化方案，CVNRD也是一个下界障碍。

Result: 证明了对任意实值编码C ⊆ ℝ≥0^m，存在大小近似线性于CVNRD的(1±ε)-稀疏化器；同时，对于坐标方向上无偏的随机稀疏化方案，CVNRD也构成了稀疏化器大小的下界。

Conclusion: 该工作统一了组合稀疏化与连续稀疏化的理论，表明二者本质上是同一类稀疏化问题的不同特例，且都受CVNRD这一核心参数控制。这为后续更广泛的稀疏化研究提供了统一的分析工具。

Abstract: We study the sparsifiability of \emph{real-valued codes}, a unifying abstraction that generalizes both combinatorial and continuous notions of sparsification, including spectral sparsification. In our setting, a code $C \subseteq \mathbb{R}_{\geq 0}^m$ is simply a collection of nonnegative real-valued vectors, and for a parameter $ε> 0$, a \emph{$(1 \pm ε)$-sparsifier} of $C$ is a subset $T \subseteq [m]$, together with weights $w \in \mathbb{R}_{\geq 0}^T$, such that, for every $c \in C$, $\sum_{i \in T} w_i c_i \in (1 \pm ε)\sum_{i=1}^m c_i$. When $C \subseteq \{0,1\}^m$, this specializes to code sparsification, and hence captures CSP sparsification, as studied by Khanna--Putterman--Sudan (SODA 2024, STOC 2025) and Brakensiek--Guruswami (STOC 2025). Similarly, for a graph $G=(V,E)$, if one defines $C=\{c^{(x)}:x\in\mathbb R^V\}\subseteq\mathbb R_{\geq 0}^E$ by $c^{(x)}_{(u,v)}=(x_u-x_v)^2$, then sparsifying $C$ is exactly spectral graph sparsification, as studied by Spielman--Teng (SICOMP 2011).
  Although the techniques driving combinatorial and continuous sparsification have traditionally been largely disjoint, our main result is a single structural theorem governing the sparsifiability of arbitrary real-valued codes $C\subseteq\mathbb{R}_{\geq 0}^m$. The central parameter is \emph{continuous-valued non-redundancy} ($\mathrm{CVNRD}$), a real-valued analogue of non-redundancy that captures the largest approximately block-diagonal obstruction contained in $C$. Our theorem gives sparsifiers of size nearly-linear in $\mathrm{CVNRD}$, and shows that $\mathrm{CVNRD}$ is also a lower-bound obstruction for the broad class of coordinate-wise unbiased randomized sparsification schemes.

</details>


### [16] [Revisiting Real-Time Interval and Throughput Maximization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16163)
*Allan Borodin,Changdao He,Nadim Mottu*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文研究了实时调度中作业吞吐量最大化问题，特别是将区间调度结果扩展到更一般的吞吐量问题。讨论了无权重和比例权重情况下的常数竞争比算法，引入了提前通知的新模型，并证明了在有限不同处理时间情况下的竞争比下界和算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解区间调度的结果在多大程度能扩展到更一般的实时吞吐量最大化问题，探索不同权重函数和模型设定下的竞争比界限。

Method: 采用竞争比分析方法，针对无权重、比例权重、C-Benevolent权重函数等不同情况，设计基于抢占重启或提前通知的在线调度算法，并给出确定性下界证明。

Result: 比例权重下存在常数竞争比算法（使用抢占重启）；C-Benevolent权重可扩展；提前通知模型下无需抢占即可获常数比；但此结果不适用于所有Benevolent函数；无权重情况下，当处理时间种类不限时不存在常数竞争比，限定k种时有1/(2k)竞争比算法。

Conclusion: 区间调度结果向一般吞吐量问题的扩展是有限度的：比例权重和某些良好权重函数可扩展，但无权重通用情形无法获得常数竞争比，提前通知模型也有其适用范围限制。

Abstract: Job throughput maximization is the central maximization problem in scheduling. Interval scheduling is the special case of throughput maximization when jobs are intervals and therefore there is no slack available in which to schedule a job. It is interesting to know to what extent results for interval scheduling can be extended to the more general throughput problem in the real-time model. For the unweighted and proportionally weighted throughput problem (where the weight or value $w_i$ of a job $J_i$ is its processing time $p_i$), there are constant competitive real-time scheduling algorithms using preemption with restarting. More generally, the result for proportionally weighted interval scheduling can be extended to C-Benevolent weight functions. We also introduce a new real-time model in which jobs are announced before the actual release time of a job. We show that with sufficient advance notice, we can obtain a constant competitive ratio for proportionally weighted throughput {\it without any preemption}.
  However, this advance notice result does not extend to arbitrary C-Benevolent and D-Benevolent weight functions. Finally, we show that unlike interval scheduling, unweighted throughput using preemption with revoking admits no constant competitive ratio when the number of distinct processing times is unrestricted. More precisely, for instances with at most $k$ distinct processing times, we give a lower bound of $1/(k+1)$ and a deterministic $1/(2k)$-competitive algorithm.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有包管理工具不支持在指定时间点解析依赖关系，导致无法分析软件生态系统在发布点时的依赖状态，从而难以研究软件演化和设计动态指标（如依赖新鲜度、依赖更新节奏）。

Abstract: Dependency resolution at a specified point in time in the past can provide insight into software evolution in software ecosystems and facilitate the design of dynamic metrics (e.g., dependency freshness, dependency update rhythm). However, dependency resolution at specified points in time is not possible in major software ecosystems due to a lack of support from package management tools. The goal of this paper is to aid practitioners and researchers in analyzing the state of the ecosystem dependency graph at release points using an enriched dataset with dependency resolution at release points for npm, PyPI, and crates.io packages. In this paper, we present a methodology to construct dependency resolution at release points of packages in software ecosystems, which we enrich with vulnerability data from OSV. We apply our methodology to construct CHRONO-RESOLUTION, a dataset of dependency resolution at release points for npm, PyPI, and crates.io packages, and release it for future research.

### [18] [Two-Path Status Verification for Outbound Enterprise Messaging Pipelines: Webhook and Scheduled Polling Fallback Architecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15529)
*Devam Gupta*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种双路径状态验证架构，用于解决企业消息推送中因webhook回调失败导致CRM系统状态记录永久处于中间态的问题。主路径依赖实时webhook事件驱动更新，后备路径通过定时轮询任务调用提供商API进行状态修正，并通过幂等去重和故障检测机制保障数据一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 出站企业消息管道存在根本性的可靠性挑战：消息投递商的webhook回调可能因网络故障、端点不可用或提供商端重试耗尽而失败，导致CRM系统记录永久停留在中间状态，单一路径架构无法应对这类问题。

Method: 提出双路径状态验证架构：(1) 主路径：实时webhook经REST端点接收，发布内部事件异步更新记录；(2) 后备路径：可配置的定时轮询任务检测仍处于过渡状态的记录，直接查询提供商状态API进行状态修正。同时采用幂等upsert实现去重，并设计了同步失败检测机制，考虑了平台资源限制对设计的影响。

Result: 该架构已在多租户PaaS基础设施上的CRM原生消息系统中得到验证，能够有效避免消息状态永久丢失，保证CRM系统记录的最终一致性。

Conclusion: 双路径架构通过实时webhook与定时轮询互补，以幂等设计和故障检测为保障，能够在多租户PaaS环境下可靠地解决企业消息推送中的状态同步可靠性问题。

Abstract: Outbound enterprise messaging pipelines face a fundamental reliability challenge: delivery status callbacks (webhooks) from messaging providers are subject to network failures, endpoint unavailability, and provider-side retry exhaustion, resulting in stale status records in the CRM system of record. A naive single-path architecture that relies exclusively on webhooks leaves a population of messages permanently in an intermediate state when callbacks fail. This paper presents a two-path status verification architecture, generalized from patterns observed in production CRM-native messaging systems built on multi-tenant platform-as-a-service infrastructure. The primary path uses a real-time webhook received by a REST endpoint, which publishes an internal event for asynchronous record update. The fallback path uses a configurable scheduled polling job that detects records still in transitional status after a configurable interval and queries the provider's status API directly to reconcile state. We describe the event-driven primary path, the scheduler-based fallback, deduplication via idempotent upsert, the sync failure detection mechanism, and the platform resource-limit considerations that shape each design decision.

</details>


### [19] [Understanding Agent-Reactive Bugs at the Model-Harness Boundary: An Empirical Study of LLM Agent Issue Reports](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15684)
*Jingyi Chen,Songqiang Chen,Hengcheng Zhu,Jialun Cao,Jiasi Shen,Shing-Chi Cheung*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文首次对LLM Agent中的"智能体反应性（AR）Bug"进行了实证研究，分析了255份来自Codex、Gemini-CLI、LangChain和CrewAI的Bug报告，构建了包含症状和触发行为的两轴分类法，发现AR Bug常以无明确测试预言（Test Oracle）的静默错误形式出现，且LLM输出的随机性增加了复现难度。用户和开发者在修复策略上存在认知分歧，用户倾向在框架侧增加防护，而开发者则常归因于LLM本身。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究将Agent失败要么归因于模型能力不足，要么归因于框架侧缺陷（如API过时、配置不匹配），缺乏对"只有特定LLM响应引发框架异常反应才出现的Bug"这一交叉领域的系统性研究。

Method: 对Codex、Gemini-CLI、LangChain、CrewAI四个系统共255份Bug报告进行人工分析，构建了两轴分类法：一轴是**可观察症状**（如崩溃、静默错误、非预期行为），另一轴是**触发Bug的LLM行为**（如格式错误、内容违背约束、逻辑跳跃等）。

Result: 1）多数AR Bug表现为无明确测试预言的静默错误，检测困难；2）LLM响应的随机性导致Bug难以复现；3）用户与开发者在修复策略上存在错配：用户倾向在框架侧加防护（如输入验证、重试机制），而开发者可能归因于LLM或对用户建议响应缓慢。

Conclusion: AR Bug对LLM Agent系统构成独特挑战，亟需针对性的测试预言设计、Bug复现支持工具及故障定位技术。

Abstract: LLM agents span command-line interfaces (e.g., Codex) and agent frameworks (e.g., LangChain), integrating backend LLMs with harness code that parses model outputs, controls agent loops, and manages context. Both the harness and LLM-generated responses jointly shape an agent's execution. This architecture gives rise to bugs that cannot be readily understood by inspecting either component alone, because some bugs occur only when a particular LLM response elicits an abnormal reaction from the agent. Prior empirical studies of agent bugs have largely attributed failures either to limited model capabilities or to harness-side defects, such as outdated APIs and configuration misalignment, without characterizing these AR bugs. We conduct the first empirical study focused on agent-reactive (AR) bugs. Through manual analysis of 255 bug reports from Codex, Gemini-CLI, LangChain, and CrewAI, we construct a two-axis taxonomy covering observable symptoms and the LLM behaviors that trigger them. Our findings show that many AR bugs manifest as silent errors without well-defined test oracles, which makes detection difficult. The stochasticity of LLM responses further complicates bug reproduction. We additionally examine fixes proposed by users and implemented by developers. This analysis exposes a mismatch: users frequently advocate harness-side guardrails, whereas developers may attribute the issue to the LLM or respond slowly to user-proposed fixes. These findings point to the need for mechanisms that help users and developers understand the root causes and resolutions of AR bugs. Overall, the study highlights challenges specific to LLM agents and motivates the design of test oracles, reproduction support, and fault-localization techniques for AR bugs.

</details>


### [20] [Verified LLM-Driven Synthesis for Concept Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15718)
*Alcino Cunha*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于概念（Concept）的软件设计形式化语义，并利用CEGIS框架和大语言模型（LLM）自动合成满足安全不变性的反应（Reaction）设计。研究比较了仅靠不变性约束、自然语言提示、正/负场景引导以及LLM驱动的场景启发等多种设计引导方式，实验表明场景引导比自然语言提示更一致，但存在过拟合和覆盖不全的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 概念设计将软件系统围绕用户面向的、自包含的功能单元（概念）进行组织，并通过同步规则（反应）组合成应用。然而，如何自动验证这些反应设计的安全不变性，以及如何在满足不变性的前提下引导合成朝向用户意图，是当前面临的关键挑战。

Method: 论文首先为概念和反应给出了形式化语义，支持安全不变性的自动验证；然后提出了一种CEGIS风格、LLM驱动的反应设计合成方法；最后研究了三种设计引导策略：仅靠不变性、自然语言提示和正/负场景，并提出了LLM驱动的场景启发技术。

Result: 在三个应用和十二个设计变体上的实验表明：仅靠不变性合成虽然快速但设计不一致且常出现不合理结果；场景引导比自然语言提示更一致地恢复预期设计，但最小场景可能导致过拟合；LLM驱动的场景启发在多数变体中能恢复预期设计，但行为遗漏和非确定性阻碍了全覆盖。

Conclusion: 不变性约束单独不足以确定设计意图，需要额外的引导信号。场景引导在一致性上优于自然语言提示，但场景的质量和覆盖范围至关重要。LLM驱动的场景启发降低了用户编写成本，但仍需进一步解决覆盖完备性问题。

Abstract: Concept Design structures software systems around concepts: user-facing, self-contained units of functionality with a focused purpose. Concepts are composed into applications using synchronization rules called reactions, which specify how actions in one concept trigger actions in others. This paper first gives a formal semantics for concepts and reactions, enabling automatic verification of safety invariants in applications developed with this methodology. It then presents a CEGIS-style, LLM-driven synthesis procedure for generating reaction designs that satisfy such invariants. Because many different designs can satisfy the same invariant, we study two ways of steering synthesis toward the user's intended design: natural-language prompts and positive/negative scenarios. We also propose an LLM-driven scenario elicitation technique to support early design exploration. In an evaluation on three applications and twelve design variants using one LLM configuration, invariant-only synthesis reached verified designs quickly but often produced inconsistent designs across runs, some of which were implausible, showing that invariants alone underconstrain the design task. Scenario-guided synthesis recovered intended designs more consistently than natural-language prompting, although minimal scenarios can lead to overfitting. LLM-driven scenario elicitation, where the user classifies proposed scenarios rather than authoring them from scratch, recovered the intended designs in most variants when enough scenarios were elicited, but missed behaviors and non-determinism prevented reliable coverage in all cases.

### [21] [GapForge: Directed Compiler Fuzzing via Coverage-Gap Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15762)
*Mingxuan Zhu,Qingyuan Liang,Junjie Chen,Zhihong Xue,Dan Hao*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: GapForge提出了一种基于LLM的编译器测试生成技术，通过覆盖间隙感知、路径差异分析和迭代提示合成，显著提升了GCC和LLVM核心模块的代码覆盖率，并发现了12个真实编译器缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有编译器测试生成技术（包括白盒方法）在大规模编译器上覆盖率有限，许多难以触及的边缘区域长期存在测试盲区，导致编译器缺陷在版本迭代中持续存活。

Method: 三步法：(1) 基于覆盖率的文件优先级评分；(2) 对未覆盖行进行路径差异分析，推断触发条件；(3) 合成针对性提示，并利用反馈迭代优化。

Result: 在GCC 14.3.0和LLVM 19.1.0上，核心模块覆盖率分别达到68.13%和69.11%，比WhiteFox多覆盖24,736和19,798行代码；发现12个真实编译器缺陷（5个GCC、7个LLVM），包括8个崩溃和4个误编译。

Conclusion: 将覆盖间隙作为显式区域级目标，结合LLM的代码生成能力与细粒度路径分析，是突破编译器测试覆盖率瓶颈的有效途径，各组件对整体性能均有贡献。

Abstract: Modern compiler codebases (e.g., GCC and LLVM) are large and complex, making comprehensive coverage across diverse code regions highly challenging. Most existing test generation techniques ignore characteristics of the target code, producing test programs that exercise only a limited subset of it. Consequently, substantial compiler regions remain insufficiently tested, leaving persistent long-tail coverage gaps that survive across releases. Even existing white-box techniques achieve limited coverage on large-scale compilers. To improve compiler coverage, especially for hard-to-reach edge regions, we present GapForge, a targeted LLM-based test generation technique that reasons about coverage gaps. Unlike program-driven techniques that generate diverse inputs without modeling which regions they exercise, and unlike whole-file summarization that yields coarse guidance, GapForge treats coverage gaps as explicit region-level targets in three steps. First, it prioritizes files via coverage-driven scoring that favors large, undercovered files. Second, it pairs each uncovered line span with its enclosing covered context and performs path-difference analysis to infer fine-grained triggering requirements: the program structures and compilation options needed to reach the uncovered region. Third, it synthesizes prompts from these requirements and previously failed prompts, using coverage feedback to guide next-round selection. On GCC 14.3.0 and LLVM 19.1.0, GapForge significantly outperforms eight state-of-the-art techniques. Within 72 hours, it achieves 68.13% and 69.11% coverage on core compiler modules in GCC and LLVM, surpassing the white-box technique WhiteFox by 24,736 and 19,798 additional lines, respectively. Moreover, GapForge discovers 12 real-world compiler failures (5 in GCC, 7 in LLVM), including 8 crashes and 4 miscompilations, with each component contributing to its performance.

</details>


### [22] [Making Agent-Mediated Contributions Governable: A Project-Level Governance Manifest for Open-Source AI Collaboration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15769)
*Jinjin Gao,Luyang Li,Shufen Guo,Ligang He,Xiaoning Sun*

TL;DR: 本文针对生成式AI与编码代理加剧开源软件治理难题的现状，提出项目侧"可治理性基础设施"理论，并开发了"代理治理清单"（AGM）作为边界资源与双向治理契约。通过50个GitHub仓库审计发现缺乏全局治理协调，实验验证AGM在风险标签恢复和评审支持方面显著优于基线。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 对50个GitHub仓库进行诊断审计，发现治理基础设施碎片化；2) 提出"项目侧可治理性基础设施"理论；3) 开发代理治理清单（AGM）作为仓库托管的边界资源与双向治理契约；4) 进行评审侧受控实验（15人，75个任务级输出）和贡献侧可行性验证（15人，45个任务）。

Result: 评审侧：AGM支持的材料在精确风险标签恢复（37/38 vs 15/37）和感知评审支持（6.14 vs 3.27，7分制）上显著优于基线。贡献侧：所有最终包正确表示核心治理状态，41个通过严格结构验证。

Conclusion: 研究构建了可读性、可追溯性、可治理性三层框架，将代理中介贡献理论化为"可治理边界对象"，推动合规型数字创新治理，同时维护维护者的决策权威。

Abstract: Generative AI and coding agents are intensifying a central governance tension in open-source software (OSS): they scale contribution generation faster than maintainers can assess risk, evidence, and accountability. Existing responses improve agent-readability and traceability, but project rules must also organize contribution-specific risk, evidence, accountability, and review-gate states. We theorize this organizational arrangement as project-side governability infrastructure. A diagnostic audit of 50 GitHub repositories finds widespread general governance artifacts, observable agent-readability, and fragmented AI-governance cues, but no project-wide arrangement that coordinates shared rules, preparation obligations, verification rights, and maintainer decision authority across AI-mediated contribution workflows. We develop the Agent Governance Manifest (AGM) as a repository-hosted boundary resource and bidirectional governance contract linking contributor-side evidence preparation with maintainer-side verification. In a controlled reviewer-side evaluation with 15 participants and 75 task-level outputs, AGM-supported materials improved exact risk-label recovery (37/38 vs. 15/37) and perceived review support (6.14 vs. 3.27 on a 1-7 scale). In a contributor-side feasibility check, 15 participants completed 45 tasks; all final packages represented the core governance state correctly, and 41 passed strict structural validation. The study develops a three-layer framework of agent-readability, traceability, and governability, theorizes agent-mediated contributions as governable boundary objects, and advances compliance-enabling digital innovation governance while preserving maintainer decision authority.

### [23] [READU: Inconsistency-Driven Just-in-Time Detection and Repair of README Bugs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15780)
*Doehyun Baek,Kilian Krampf,Michael Pradel*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: READU是一个基于不一致性检测的自动化工具，能够在提交时即时发现并修复README文档中的错误（README bugs），通过在六个流行仓库的6000个提交上达到75%的精度和217个自动修复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 仓库级文档（如README）是用户与仓库的第一接触点，但文档中的错误会导致用户运行时错误或浪费时间调试。修复这类错误很困难，因为文档混合了散文和代码、与真实来源关联松散，且发现错误后仍需开发者手动修复。

Method: READU通过检测文档与两类事实源（仓库内部事实如源代码、仓库外部事实如外部依赖）之间的不一致来发现README bugs。具体流程包括：高召回率提交过滤器、并行运行内部和外部一致性检查器、使用警报判断器去除误报、自动合成文档补丁。

Result: 在六个流行仓库（包括Linux和Spring Boot）的6000个近期提交上，READU检测出244个真阳性，精度75%，每次提交平均消耗不到0.01美元和不到一分钟。其中217个真阳性被正确修复。已报告66个发现的README bugs，44个被确认，26个已修复。

Conclusion: 不一致性驱动的方法能有效检测和修复README文档错误，实现了较高的精度和自动化修复率，且成本极低，具有实用价值。

Abstract: Repository-level documentation, such as READMEs, is often the first point of contact between users and a repository. When this documentation is incorrect, users may encounter runtime errors or waste their time debugging. We call such mistakes in repository-level documentation README bugs. Addressing README bugs is challenging because documentation mixes prose with code, its connection to the source of truth is loose, and finding a bug still leaves developers to craft a repair. This paper presents READU, an inconsistency-driven technique for just-in-time detection and repair of README bugs. The key insight behind READU is that README bugs often manifest as inconsistencies between documentation and another source of truth: either repository-internal facts, such as source code, or repository-external facts, such as external dependencies. READU applies a high-recall commit filter, runs internal and external consistency checkers in parallel, uses an alert judge to remove false positives, and automatically synthesizes documentation patches. On 6,000 recent commits from six popular repositories including Linux and Spring Boot, READU detects 244 true positives with 75% precision, while consuming less than $0.01 and less than one minute per commit, on average. Of these true positives, READU correctly repairs 217. We report 66 found README bugs, of which (so far) 44 are confirmed and 26 are fixed.

</details>


### [24] [In the Driver's Seat: A Multi-Company Study on the Reality of Autonomous Driving System Testing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15820)
*Qunying Song,Yuan Gao,Johannes Betz,Dietmar Pfahl,Mohammad Reza Mousavi,Federica Sarro*

TL;DR: 通过对9家不同国家公司的专家访谈，该研究总结了自动驾驶系统测试的行业实践、挑战与未来趋势，并提出了一个以证据为中心的闭环测试框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动驾驶系统快速发展并投入实际应用，但缺乏完善的测试标准（场景选择、性能评估、验收标准等），亟需深入了解行业测试实践与挑战。

Method: 采用访谈研究方法，对来自6个国家9家公司的自动驾驶开发与测试专家进行深度访谈，并通过主题分析法对数据进行提炼和归纳。

Result: 当前实践以场景测试和X-in-the-loop测试为主；主要挑战包括场景真实性、场景覆盖率、仿真保真度和验收标准；专家提出AI、世界模型和端到端方法等潜在解决方案；未来趋势是自动化、数据驱动和行业透明化。

Conclusion: 研究提供了行业扎根的ADS测试全景图，提出了以证据为中心的闭环测试框架，为实践提供了行动指南，并为未来研究方向指明了道路。

Abstract: Autonomous driving systems (ADS) are rapidly advancing and increasingly deployed in real-world applications. This creates growing demands for effective testing to ensure system functionality and safety. However, ADS testing remains complex and lacks well-established standards for scenario selection, performance evaluation, and acceptance criteria. To better understand current ADS testing practices and challenges, we conducted an interview study with experts working on ADS development and testing in nine companies from six different countries. Through thematic analysis, we synthesized industrial testing practices, challenges, potential solutions, future trends, and proposed an evidence-centered closed-loop testing framework for ADS testing. Our findings show that current practices primarily focus on scenario-based and X-in-the-loop testing approaches, supported by diverse tools, metrics, benchmarks, and testing strategies. The participants highlighted major challenges related to scenario realism, scenario coverage, simulation fidelity, and acceptance criteria, while also discussing potential solutions such as the use of AI, world models, and end-to-end approaches. Furthermore, participants envisioned future ADS testing to become more automated, data-driven, and transparent across the industry. Overall, this study provides a comprehensive industry-grounded overview of ADS testing, proposes an evidence-centered closed-loop testing framework to provide actionable guidance for ADS testing, and outlines important directions for future research and practice.

### [25] [Agentic Synthesis against Counterexample-Supplemented Sketches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15854)
*Muness Castle,Eric Rubeck*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为"针对反例补充草稿的智能体合成"（Agentic Synthesis against Counterexample-Supplemented Sketches）的仓库原生方法，用于在实现过程中发现治理策略的编码系统。人类从部分代码草稿开始，编码智能体生成初始实现；当具体失败暴露缺失或错误的策略时，操作员明确批准修正后的行为和规则。该方法通过CatSynth合成浏览器应用进行了演示，实验表明从演化草稿重建比从初始草稿重放所有示例效果更好，能够减少重复工作并携带已审查的策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前编码智能体在修复失败示例时可能无法保留导致失败的领域规则，导致后续生成重复相同的错误。需要一种方法让系统在实现过程中发现并巩固治理策略。

Method: 提出"针对反例补充草稿的智能体合成"方法：人类提供部分代码草稿→智能体生成初始实现→遇到具体失败时操作员批准修正行为和规则→智能体根据反例修订草稿并修复/重新生成代码→完整归档保存溯源→回归测试集把关每次修订→定期从演化草稿而不是提示历史或累积示例中重新生成。

Result: 在CatSynth实验（使用GPT-5.4-mini）中：8/14冻结候选案例成为反例；从演化草稿重建通过19/21保留案例（优于初始草稿重放所有示例的15/21）；跨反例保留代码只需9次Developer调用和719行累积产物变更（对比重放所有需15次调用和2394行），并通过18/21保留案例。

Conclusion: 演化草稿成功携带了已审查的策略，保留代码减少了返工量。但该结果基于单一模型和单一揭示顺序，不能确立普遍优越性或超越编码检查的正确性。

Abstract: Coding agents can fix a failing example without preserving the domain rule that made it fail, so later generations can repeat the same plausible mistake. We present agentic synthesis against counterexample-supplemented sketches, a repository-native method for systems whose governing policy is discovered during implementation. A human starts with a partial, code-shaped sketch, and a coding agent generates the first implementation. When a concrete failure exposes missing or mistaken policy, an operator explicitly approves the corrected behavior and rule. The agent then revises the sketch and repairs or regenerates code and prompt surfaces for that one counterexample. The full archive preserves provenance; a selected regression set gates each revision before the next candidate is revealed; and periodic clean regeneration tests whether the evolved sketch, rather than prompt history or accumulated examples, carries the learned policy.
  We demonstrate the method with CatSynth, a synthetic browser application and captured coding-agent experiment. In one open-world run with GPT-5.4-mini, 8 of 14 frozen candidate cases became counterexamples. The rebuild controls inherited that promotion schedule, and all three paths passed the 8 accepted cases. Rebuilding from the evolved sketch passed 19 of 21 withheld cases, compared with 15 of 21 when rebuilding from the initial sketch and replaying all accepted examples. Retaining code across counterexamples required 9 Developer calls and 719 lines of cumulative artifact churn, versus 15 calls and 2,394 lines for replay-all, and passed 18 of 21 withheld cases. These results provide inspectable evidence that the evolved sketch carried reviewed policy and that retaining code reduced rework in this run; with one model and one reveal order, they do not establish general superiority or correctness beyond the encoded checks.

</details>


### [26] [Trans-Domain Digital Twin: Conceptual Foundations, Architecture, and Research Outlook](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15908)
*Mansoorali Amiri*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出跨域数字孪生（Trans-Domain Digital Twin）框架，通过七层概念架构、编排核心、最小合规条件及渐进式快-中-慢循环等机制，实现异质领域间状态、误差、目标、约束、决策和控制的显式耦合与协同操作，并建立了从离线训练到有界在线适应的运行范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出七层概念架构、跨域编排核心、最小合规条件、通用操作形式化、渐进式快-中-慢循环、单回合离线训练与有界在线自适应机制，并给出概念验证与评估标准、成熟度模型、参考部署架构及运行时安全、溯源、版本管理和模型生命周期管理要求。

Result: 该框架在概念层面可与数字孪生、模型交换、分布式仿真和智能传感器等标准映射；但其形式合规性和操作有效性仍需通过独立基准测试、不确定性量化、消融实验和现场验证来检验。

Conclusion: 跨域数字孪生为复合/联邦数字孪生系统提供了一种操作化形式，但当前尚处于概念提出阶段，需进一步通过实证研究验证其有效性。

Abstract: Complex systems comprise heterogeneous domains whose states, uncertainties, risks, and control consequences can cross domain boundaries. Existing cross-domain digital twin approaches broadly focus on comparison, reuse, semantic mapping, standardization, and interoperability, but do not inherently require operational connections among domain states, errors, objectives, constraints, decisions, and controls. This article proposes the trans-domain digital twin as an operational formulation along the continuum of Composite/Federated Digital Twin Systems. This approach connects heterogeneous domain twins through an aligned shared state, explicit coupling of data, models, states, errors, objectives, and controls, heterogeneous temporal coordination, joint decision-making, and feedback-based adaptation. The proposed framework presents a seven-layer conceptual architecture, a trans-domain orchestration core, minimum compliance conditions, a general operational formalism, progressive fast-meso-slow loops, and a single-episode offline training mechanism linked to bounded online adaptation. It also describes conceptual validation and evaluation criteria, a maturity model, a reference deployment architecture, and requirements for runtime safety, provenance, versioning, and model lifecycle management. The framework is conceptually mappable to standards for digital twins, model exchange, distributed simulation, and smart transducers; however, its formal compliance and operational effectiveness must be examined through independent benchmarks, uncertainty quantification, ablation testing, and field validation.

### [27] [TARS: A Theory-of-Mind Agent for Personalized In-IDE Code Comprehension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15948)
*Leopoldo Todisco,Antonio Della Porta,Stefano Lambiase,Fabio Palomba*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: TARS是一个集成在VS Code中的LLM智能代理，通过轻量级心智理论范式对开发者进行画像，自适应调整代码解释的深度和语气，并利用RAG技术参考项目文档。实验表明，使用TARS的开发者任务完成速度提升26%，认知负荷更低，且解释质量更高。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 代码理解是软件工程中最耗时的任务之一，现有LLM助手的解释忽视用户身份，迫使开发者采用破坏性的复制-粘贴工作流，缺乏个性化和上下文感知能力。

Method: 提出TARS系统：1) 基于轻量级心智理论范式构建开发者画像（专业知识、角色、风格偏好）；2) 通过RAG检索项目文档来支撑解释；3) 自适应调整解释的深度和语气；4) 集成到VS Code中，直接在代码上提供锚定解释。

Result: 通过18名参与者在非平凡Java代码片段上的对照实验，使用TARS的参与者任务完成速度快26%，认知负荷更低，且认为解释能够根据其画像进行有意义的自适应调整。

Conclusion: TARS通过个性化和上下文感知的代码解释方式，显著提升了开发者的代码理解效率并降低了认知负荷，验证了将心智理论和RAG技术结合用于代码理解助手的有效性。

Abstract: Code comprehension is one of the most time-consuming tasks in software engineering, yet most LLM-based assistants produce explanations that ignore who is asking and force developers into a disruptive copy-paste workflow. We present TARS, an LLM-powered agent integrated into Visual Studio Code that supports program comprehension through autonomous explanations anchored directly to the code under analysis. Built around a lightweight Theory of Mind paradigm, TARS profiles a developer's expertise, role, and stylistic preferences, then adapts the depth and tone of its explanations accordingly, grounding them in project documentation via Retrieval-Augmented Generation. To evaluate TARS, we conducted a controlled experiment with 18 participants on non-trivial Java snippets. Participants using TARS completed tasks 26\% faster, reported lower cognitive load, and found the explanations meaningfully adapted to their profiles.

### [28] [DiffTestGen: Change-Directed LLM-Based Testing for Exposing Behavioral Differences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16024)
*Huimin Hu,Cristian Cadar,Michael Pradel*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: DiffTestGen是一种基于LLM的变化导向差分测试方法，利用静态调用图分析和项目文档生成能触发新旧版本行为差异的测试用例，在463个PR中78.2%成功暴露行为差异，平均联合覆盖率达90.7%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 软件演化过程中需要确保行为变更符合开发者意图，但现有方法无法有效触发许多代码变更中的行为差异，导致回归缺陷难以检测。

Method: 1) 利用静态调用图分析和项目文档识别有效的测试入口点，引导LLM到达变更代码；2) 提出联合覆盖度量（union coverage metric），结合新旧版本修改代码的覆盖率，通过迭代反馈优化LLM生成测试。

Result: 在463个PR上，DiffTestGen在78.2%的PR中暴露行为差异，平均联合覆盖率达90.7%；相比基线多暴露99个PR，代码覆盖率提升12.5%和15.6个百分点；集成Testora后可检测到现有方法遗漏的回归缺陷。

Conclusion: DiffTestGen有效提升了变化导向测试中行为差异的暴露能力，联合覆盖度量是指导LLM生成有效测试的关键，具有检测回归缺陷的实际应用价值。

Abstract: As software evolves over time, it is important to ensure that any behavioral changes occur as intended by developers. A promising approach for this goal is to generate tests that expose behavioral differences between the old and new versions of a program. However, current approaches fail to trigger behavioral differences for many code changes. This paper presents~DiffTestGen, a novel change-directed, LLM-based differential testing approach specifically designed to expose behavioral differences introduced by a code change. The approach is enabled by two key contributions: First, DiffTestGen leverages static call graph analysis and project documentation to identify valid entry points for test generation and to guide the LLM toward reaching the changed code. Second, DiffTestGen iteratively improves our newly introduced union coverage metric, which combines coverage of modified code in the old and the new version, by providing targeted coverage feedback to the LLM. We evaluate DiffTestGen on two datasets comprising a total of 463 PRs. DiffTestGen exposes behavioral differences in 78.2% of the PRs while achieving an average union coverage of 90.7%. Compared with the baselines, DiffTestGen exposes 99 more PRs overall and increases code coverage by 12.5% and 15.6% percentage points, respectively. By integrating DiffTestGen with the Testora regression detector, we show that the identified behavioral differences can be used to detect regression bugs missed by the best existing approaches.

</details>

*Danilo Monteiro Ribeiro,Ronnie de Souza Santos,Rodrigo Siqueira,Breno Andrade,Rafael Batista Duarte,Gilberto Hida,Julia Alencar,Gustavo Pinto*

Result: 识别出八项能力：领域专业与AI输出监督（123篇）、元认知与AI使用决策（55篇）、伦理与学术诚信（53篇）、科研提示工程（38篇）、AI使用可复现性（29篇）、AI素养与技术知识（16篇）等，其中领域专业知识被视为批判性评估的前提条件。

Abstract: The growing adoption of Large Language Models in scientific research has created a need to understand what competencies researchers and graduate students require to use these tools critically and responsibly. This rapid review analyzed 194 articles retrieved from Elicit and Google Scholar (2022 to 2025), from which 40 were selected for competency extraction and thematic analysis following independent dual screening (Gwet AC1: 0.76 to 0.83). Eight competencies were identified. The most prevalent was domain expertise and oversight of AI outputs (n = 123), encompassing subject matter mastery, systematic skepticism, source verification, and researcher accountability. Other key competencies include metacognition and decision making about AI use (n = 55), ethics and academic integrity (n = 53), prompt engineering for research (n = 38), and reproducibility of AI use (n = 29). AI literacy and technical knowledge (n = 16) was explicitly identified as a risk factor when absent, with domain expertise treated as a prerequisite for meaningful critical evaluation. The findings suggest that preparing researchers to use LLMs goes beyond technical instruction, requiring an integrated set of epistemic, ethical, and methodological competencies centered on human accountability for the knowledge produced. These results have direct implications for the design of graduate programs and AI literacy initiatives.

In this study, we aim to address this issue by evaluating five preselected software tools-REMix, MTRESS, COMANDO, OEMOF, and HOMER PRO-to identify the scenarios for which they are most suitable. ### [31] [ADASCALE: An Adaptive Scaling and Placement Framework for Microservices Under Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15681)
*Ming Chen,Muhammed Tawfiqul Islam,Maria Rodriguez Read,Rajkumar Buyya*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: ADASCALE提出了一种自适应框架，在云-边环境中对微服务副本进行联合扩缩容与放置，通过MAPE循环感知多维动态（异构节点、时变延迟、非平稳流量、混合根操作），并相比NetMARKS_Scale实现了最高1.93倍的平均响应时间降低和2.16倍的吞吐量提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动扩缩器与网络感知调度器通常只处理部分动态因素（如仅考虑计算瓶颈或仅考虑跨节点延迟），导致在云-边环境中出现SLO违背问题。微服务面临非平稳流量、根操作混合变化、异构通信模式等多维动态，亟需一个能联合优化扩缩容与放置决策的框架。

Method: ADASCALE基于MAPE循环：1) 从分布式追踪和服务网格指标中提取每个边缘和服务级别的需求；2) 识别混合工作负载下最关键的根操作；3) 计算SLO感知的副本目标数；4) 根据当前节点间延迟矩阵，以需求加权延迟最小化为目标放置副本。同时引入反应式放置循环应对网络扰动，稳态扩缩容循环处理需求变化。

Result: 在Cloud-Edge Kubernetes集群上使用DeathStarBench Social Network三个根操作进行测试：相比NetMARKS_Scale，compose-post、read-home-timeline、read-user-timeline平均响应时间分别降低至1.56x、1.93x、1.34x，吞吐量分别提升至2.16x、1.32x、1.36x，且始终满足SLO目标。

Conclusion: ADASCALE证明了联合优化扩缩容与放置决策在云-边环境多维动态下的有效性，能同时保障SLO、降低延迟并提升吞吐量。

Abstract: Microservice applications are increasingly deployed across cloud--edge environments, where heterogeneous nodes and time-varying inter-node delays amplify the impact of placement decisions. At the same time, these applications face non-stationary traffic, shifts in the mix of root request operations that exercise different call graphs, and heterogeneous communication modes that determine how network latency and queuing propagate to end-to-end (E2E) performance. Existing autoscalers and network-aware schedulers typically handle only a subset of these dynamics, leading to either compute bottlenecks or inflated cross-node latency and thus SLO violations.
  We propose ADASCALE, an adaptive framework that jointly scales and places microservice replicas under such multi-dimensional dynamics. ADASCALE implements a Monitor--Analyzer--Planner--Executor (MAPE) loop that extracts per-edge and per-service demand from distributed traces and service-mesh metrics, identifies the most critical root operation under a mixed workload, computes SLO-aware replica targets, and then places replicas to minimize a demand-weighted latency objective given the current inter-node latency matrix. To react quickly to networking perturbations, ADASCALE triggers a reactive placement loop, while a steady-state autoscaling loop handles demand shifts.
  We evaluate ADASCALE on a cloud--edge Kubernetes cluster using the DeathStarBench Social Network application with three root operations under varying load and workload mixes. Across scenarios, ADASCALE consistently meets SLO targets and improves both latency and throughput: compared with NetMARKS_Scale, it achieves up to 1.56x, 1.93x, and 1.34x lower average response time (for compose-post, read-home-timeline, and read-user-timeline) and up to 2.16x, 1.32x, and 1.36x higher throughput, respectively.

</details>


### [32] [Split-Aware Function Placement with Availability Guarantees and Optical Provisioning in vRANs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15816)
*Mayank Ramnani,Shasank Dixit,Sushil Yadav,Saad Ahmed,Sidharth Sharma*

Main category: cs.NI

Method: 将问题建模为整数线性规划（ILP）模型，包含两种变体：非共享备份方案和更经济的共享备份方案。为应对ILP计算复杂度，开发了启发式算法和基于遗传算法（GA）的元启发式算法，在满足延迟、处理、带宽和可用性约束下最大化运营商利润。

Result: 在最多128个节点的拓扑上进行评估，共享备份方案相比非共享方案利润提升高达18%，归一化CPU使用率降低5-10%，且遗传算法能在实时获得近优解。

Conclusion: 共享备份机制在解耦vRAN中能有效平衡可靠性与成本，所提出的集成框架和元启发式算法为未来6G网络的切片感知、功能分割感知的资源优化提供了可行的实践方案。

Abstract: The rapid evolution of beyond-5G and emerging 6G networks is driving the need for flexible, reliable, and cost-efficient virtualized Radio Access Network (vRAN) architectures capable of supporting heterogeneous services such as enhanced Mobile Broadband (eMBB), Ultra-Reliable Low-Latency Communication (URLLC), and Massive Machine-Type Communication (mMTC). Future disaggregated RAN systems are expected to rely heavily on network slicing, functional split flexibility, and optical x-haul infrastructures to support stringent performance, scalability, and availability requirements. In this paper, we present an integrated framework for reliable, slice-aware, and functional split-aware Virtual Network Function (VNF) placement with lightpath provisioning in disaggregated vRAN environments. The proposed approach maximizes mobile network operators' profit by jointly optimizing function placement and optical resource allocation under latency, processing, bandwidth, and availability constraints. We formulate the problem as an Integer Linear Programming (ILP) model with two variants: one that employs unshared backups and another that uses a more cost-efficient shared backup scheme. To address ILP complexity, we develop a heuristic algorithm and a Genetic Algorithm (GA)-based metaheuristic that yields near-optimal solutions in real time. Extensive evaluations on topologies up to 128 nodes show that shared backup variants yield up to 18% higher profit, while maintaining up to 5-10% lower normalized CPU usage than unshared counterparts.

### [33] [App-Based Performance Characterization of Cellular and Wi-Fi Networks in Dense Stadium Deployments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16008)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The concentration of 77,622 spectators during football games at Notre Dame Stadium creates an exceptionally demanding environment for wireless infrastructure. To handle this extreme user density, the stadium deploys concurrent multi-tier networks serving outdoor users: an enterprise 5/6 GHz Wi-Fi network with ~900 outdoor Access Points (APs) alongside high-density multi-carrier 4G/5G networks powered by a neutral-host small-cell Distributed Antenna System (DAS) with up to 129 unique cell identifiers (PCIs) per operator. This study evaluates user-perceived performance and QoE across these networks using commercial smartphones to execute web browsing, WhatsApp messaging, and Instagram media posting workloads. Our empirical results reveal that while cellular networks deliver strong peak downlink performance in an empty stadium, game-day crowd loads heavily strain uplink and latency performance, triggering a severe cellular "uplink gap." Under Non-Standalone (EN-DC) anchor congestion, web browsing handshakes suffer a catastrophic 5,983 ms P90 Time-to-First-Byte (TTFB), and image upload failure rates climb to 46%. Furthermore, while narrow low-band FDD channels (e.g., n5) maintain robust channel quality during uploads, they exhibit a 70% median Block Error Rate (BLER) during active browsing tests, driving a 36.6% page-load failure rate. Conversely, the dense stadium Wi-Fi infrastructure delivers downlink throughput comparable to the best performing 5G Standalone (SA) deployment while providing better uplink and latency resilience, yielding the lowest game-day page-load failure rate (3.9%) and bounding image upload latency degradation to just 2.1x relative to empty-stadium baselines. These insights proves that densification through localized Wi-Fi deployment is essential to absorb severe stadium traffic spikes.

### [35] [Structure of the Circular-Dyadic Convolution Error](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15293)
*Ben Fauber,Alireza Moradzadeh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了用Hadamard变换替代FFT计算循环卷积时产生的代数误差，发现误差具有结构化特征：两个位置完全无误差、误差算子接近满秩但零空间维度对数增长、期望误差由对齐标量决定且渐进加倍输出能量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Hadamard变换具有实数值符号翻转的优势，但替代FFT会引入代数误差，作者希望系统性地刻画这一误差的结构与性质。

Method: 通过理论分析给出三个互补结果：误差精确抵消的位置识别、误差算子的秩分析、以及随机滤波器平均下的误差封闭表达式。

Result: 1) 两个输入和两个输出位置完全无误差，且无法通过输出重排消除；2) 误差算子几乎满秩，零空间仅对数维度；3) 期望误差由对齐标量控制，渐近使输出能量加倍（零误差子空间除外）。

Conclusion: 替代误差是结构化的、可预测的、由对齐机制控制的，并非随机噪声。

Abstract: Dyadic and circular convolution can both be computed in $O(N\log N)$ time using the Hadamard transform and the FFT-computed discrete Fourier transform (DFT), respectively. The Hadamard transform is preferable for its real-valued sign flips, yet its substitution for the DFT introduces algebraic error. We present three complementary results that characterize this error. First, we identify exact error cancellation: two input and two output positions are universally error-free, and no reordering of the output can eliminate this error. Second, the error operator is nearly full rank, while its null space has only logarithmic dimension. Third, the expected error is governed by a single alignment scalar, with a closed-form expression obtained by averaging over random filters. In general, the substitution error asymptotically doubles the output energy, except for filters in the universal zero-error subspace, which incur no error. Collectively, these results show that the substitution error is structured, predictable, and governed by alignment.

</details>


### [36] [Position: Quantum Program Generation Must Prioritize Validity Over Probabilistic Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15313)
*Junhao Song,Yu Zhou,William Knottenbelt,Yudong Cao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文论证了将大语言模型的规模缩放假设直接应用于量子电路合成是错误的，提出应从以人为中心的副驾驶转向以验证器为中心的智能体，通过层次化约束、拓扑掩码和符号代理来保证生成电路的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出从人类中心副驾驶转向验证器中心智能体，在生成过程中集成层次化约束、拓扑掩码和符号代理。

Result: 分析表明仅靠规模缩放无法弥合有效性差距，验证感知架构才是可行路径。

Conclusion: 量子程序生成应编码任务特定的量子信息规则，而非依赖单纯的模仿学习。

Abstract: The scaling hypothesis assumes that increasing model parameters yields emergent reasoning capabilities. This position paper argues that applying this probabilistic paradigm to generic quantum circuit synthesis is a directional error. Unlike natural languages, quantum circuits require strict adherence to mathematical constraints that manifest a significant syntax-semantics gap. Training on unverified quantum programs means that models learn syntax but fail to capture the physical semantics of the Hilbert space. Since the valid subset of circuit designs decays exponentially with the number of qubits, post-hoc filtering is mathematically intractable. We propose a pivot from human-centric copilots to verifier-centric agents. We integrate hierarchical constraints, topological masks, and symbolic proxies directly into generation. Our analysis suggests that scale alone cannot bridge the validity gap. Verification-aware architectures offer a viable path for modular quantum program generation. These considerations point toward generation methods that encode task-specific rules of quantum information, rather than relying on imitation alone.

### [37] [A Transportable Threshold-Based Framework for Interpretable Classification of Medical Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15394)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑盒模型缺乏可解释性和可重复性，限制了AI在医学中的采纳，亟需一种统计上可解释且临床可用的分类框架。

Result: 在Pima Indians Diabetes、Wisconsin Breast Cancer和Heart Failure Prediction三个基准数据集上分别取得0.800、0.984和0.919的AUC；通过泄漏安全的交叉验证校准分析（Brier分数、校准截距/斜率、beta校准）验证了概率可靠性。

Abstract: Black-box models limit the adoption of artificial intelligence in medicine due to their lack of interpretability and reproducibility. We introduce a statistically grounded framework that provides fully interpretable, rule-based clinical classification using the Bernoulli Naïve Bayes (BNB) model. The method applies supervised $χ^2$-guided statistical binarization to continuous variables, identifying thresholds that maximize association with clinical outcomes within the training data. This transformation allows BNB to operate effectively on continuous medical data without sacrificing its inherent transparency. The approach was evaluated on three benchmark datasets, Pima Indians Diabetes, Wisconsin Breast Cancer, and Heart Failure Prediction, achieving area-under-the-curve (AUC) scores of 0.800 for the Pima analysis, 0.984 for Wisconsin Breast Cancer, and 0.919 for Heart Failure Prediction. In addition to discrimination, probabilistic reliability was assessed using leakage-safe cross-validated calibration analysis including Brier score, calibration intercept/slope, and post-hoc beta calibration, which improved probability calibration across datasets. These results suggest that a statistically interpretable framework can achieve performance comparable to more complex models while providing explicit, clinically meaningful decision rules and calibrated risk estimates. To illustrate this transparency concretely, a complete worked example demonstrates that model inference can be reproduced using only a reference table and basic arithmetic, without access to software or proprietary tools. This work offers a practical approach to supporting trustworthy and generalizable AI in real-world healthcare settings.
